<h1></h1>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">And it shall come to pass, that in all the land, saith the God of Abraham Isaac and Jacob, two parts therein shall be cut off and die; but the third shall be left therein. (<strong>Zechariah 13:8 KJV)</strong></span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Zechariah 13:8 tells us that 2/3 of the Tribes of Jacob-Israel will  perish during the Great Tribulation.  America is Manasseh, one of the favourite Tribes of Jacob and that is why 2/3  of America will be killed in America.  The Deagle report predicts deaths of 223 M out of 330 M Americans or 67% reduction which is in line with Bible Prophecy of 2/3 or 66.67%.  America and Britain and the Commonwealth are Babylon  the Great however America will be getting a double portion of God of Abraham Isaac and Jacob’s wrath according to Revelation 18:6. </span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">The Jews are Edomites according to their own writings and not Shemites.  Edomites get their own special punishment according to the Book of Obadiah</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">In the 1925 Jewish Encyclopedia, it states “EDOM IS MODERN JEWRY.” The Jewish Ency. 1925 Ed., Vol. 5, Pg. 41.  The Jewish Almanac 1980 Pg.3 states Jews are not Israelites or Hebrews. The Pharisees, which are now the Ashkenazis, told Jesus the Messiah that they are of Abraham’s seed but were never in bondage, which can only mean one thing (John 8:33).  The Jews were never in the Exodus but rather is was the Caucasians that are the true Israelites or The Tribes of Jacob-Israel that were in bondage in Egypt. The Pharisees / Ashkenazis are descendants of Esau which mixed with other races and became known as the Edomites .</span></span></p>
<h1 style="text-align:justify"><strong><span style="font-size:26px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">FEDEX SHIPPING 100′S OF 1000′S OF BODY-BAGS</span></span></strong></h1>
<p><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">FedEx Shipping100′s of 1000′s of Body-Bags across the US .. most likely in preparation of mass deaths as the Government gets ready for mass roll-out of Covid-19 vaccines and Biden’s 100.000.000 vaccines in first 100 days in office. Take into consideration that this is just one FedEx facility.  </span></span></p>
<p><iframe frameborder="0" height="450" loading="lazy" scrolling="no" src="https://www.bitchute.com/embed/5SaeZFuDJUuY/" width="720"></iframe></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:26px"><strong>Project Pogo And Project Zyphr Have Commenced!</strong></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Tom, A Friend of David Goldberg who was murdered, continues to warn Americans to leave the USA and explain how they are planning to come for the patriots, Caucasians, intellectuals and Christians.  This is a war between the Edomite Jews, the children of the devil, and the Caucasians and Christians who are the Holy Seed of God of Abraham Isaac and Jacob and the True Tribes of Jacob surnamed Israel.  Esau-Edom is mad as Hell at his brother Jacob-Israel for taking his birthright and he is coming for his inheritance!  The US government have already started Project Pogo and Zyphr and are planning to come for all the Patriots, Intellectuals and Christians very soon.</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Tom was lucky enough to leave America and if you have any sense, Americans should FLEE America which is Babylon the Great.  God of Abraham Isaac and Jacob warned us in Jeremiah 51:6 to Flee America (Manasseh) and Ephraim (Britain and the Commonwealth) as both America and Brtiain and the Commonweath will be destroyed.    Canada and Mexico will be destroyed as a casualty of war.  Best place to go is the Middle East, either Egypt or Jordan.  The greater grander second Exodus will commence in Egypt so that my recommendation.  Do not go to an island or the coast line or on top of a moutain as there will be tsunamis and the mountains will all fall down according to Rev. 6:16.  If you cannot leave the country, Flee to the mountains away from the coasts as there will be tsunamis on both the east and west coast.</span></span></p>
<p style="text-align:justify"><span style="font-size:22px"><span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif">Time is short.  Only Messiah Jesus saves and if you have not accepted Messiah Jesus as your savior, then I encourage you to do so today and get baptised, full immersion at an age of accountability, 8 years and over. </span></span></p>
